(Paris) Foreign Minister Laval has just met with the British Chargé d'Affaires in France, Campbell, to discuss the issue of German rearmament. (Havas, 19th)

(Moscow) It was learned today that French Foreign Minister Laval has been invited to visit the Russian capital and may arrive in Moscow after the British Lord Privy Seal Eden leaves. (National Telegram, 19th)

(Moscow) Although the official response to Germany's rearmament plan has been silent, according to news today, Soviet Russia has asked French Foreign Minister Laval to come here immediately. The significance of Soviet Russia's invitation to Laval is believed here to be to consolidate friendly relations with France and to unite against Germany. Since the former French Foreign Minister Barthou adopted a collective policy, Franco-Russian relations have become increasingly friendly. Currently, Soviet officials believe that Germany's new policy affects France and Russia the most, so former allies should be able to reunite to prevent problems before they occur. (National Telegram, 19th)

(Rome) Soviet Ambassador to Italy Stein, accompanied by Trade Representative Belenky, paid a long visit to Italian Prime Minister Mussolini today. (TASS, 18th)

Content of British Protest 28

(London) The British government's note to Germany stated that the British government felt compelled to protest Germany's rearmament. After the German government announced the establishment of an air force, there was the recent declaration. This unilateral action, apart from the point of principle, also greatly increased unrest in Europe. The proposal for a meeting between British and German authorities arose from the joint Anglo-French communiqué of February 3rd and the German reply of February 14th, and the subsequent correspondence between the British and German governments. The British government believes that it is now appropriate to draw Germany's special attention to these documents. The note then listed the various documents, followed by saying that what Britain was planning was a comprehensive solution through free negotiations between Germany and other countries, to replace Section V of the Treaty of Versailles for Germany. The British government's policy was aimed at the success of this effort. The British government has concentrated its efforts in Geneva and elsewhere to achieve success in this. The German government's decision to substantially increase its army's strength beyond any previous proposals cannot facilitate the success of a broad agreement, which seeks to replace the provisions of the Treaty of Versailles with a common pledge. Moreover, if this strength remains unchanged, it will hinder the negotiation of an agreement with the major powers concerned. Even if it does not become impossible, it will become more difficult. The British government is extremely unwilling to abandon any opportunity that the visit of British cabinet members to Berlin may provide to promote general understanding. However, in this new environment, British cabinet members must, before engaging in this, draw the German government's attention to the above points and wish to obtain assurances and know that the German government still wishes this visit to become a reality in accordance with the previously agreed scope and purpose. That purpose is that the purpose of this meeting should be to discuss the points raised in the Anglo-French communiqué and move to a deeper stage. The points raised in the Anglo-French communiqué are

(1) The British government stated that if Austria's independence is endangered, it is willing to consult with other signatory countries to the Rome Agreement of February 17, 1934.

(2) Britain and France agreed that Germany and any other country's joint armaments provisions cannot unilaterally change this obligation.

(3) Britain and France agreed that what could help restore peace would be a solution through free negotiations between Germany and other countries to replace the articles in the Treaty of Versailles that restricted Germany's armaments and military strength.

(4) Britain and France believe that Germany's return to the League of Nations is essential. After receiving the British note, German Foreign Minister Neurath studied it briefly and then informed the British Ambassador in Berlin that the German government still wished Simon and Eden to visit Berlin in accordance with the previously agreed scope and purpose. (Reuter, 19th)

(London) The London newspapers all unanimously supported the British government's note to Germany protesting the rearmament. The Berlin newspapers also expressed great satisfaction. However, judging from the comments of the Paris newspapers and the opinions of semi-official circles, the entire nation of France was filled with shock and anger. The London morning newspapers all had positive comments on this note, and even the Daily Herald, the organ of the Labour Party, praised its wording and magnanimity. Several newspaper editorials expressed satisfaction that Germany had not closed the door to continued negotiations, but said that although Foreign Secretary Simon would go to Berlin to discuss everything with German leader Hitler and others in accordance with the previously agreed scope and purpose, it would not be easy to harmonize Hitler's declarations with the proposals contained in last month's Anglo-French communiqué. Berlin believed that the British note could bring Germany closer to other countries and regarded Foreign Secretary Simon's continued visit to Germany as a sign that international tensions had eased. According to a Reuter dispatch from Berlin, Germany expressed great satisfaction upon hearing the news that Simon would still visit Germany. The Frankfurter Zeitung welcomed the British note, calling it a pleasing expression of British common sense. The Essener National-Zeitung, the organ of Prussian Prime Minister and Aviation Minister Goering, said that since Germany is now implementing compulsory military service, the number and type of tanks, the caliber of artillery, and the strength of each other's air and naval forces can all be discussed in Berlin. According to a Reuter dispatch from Paris, the French newspapers' comments on the British note often used words such as "weak" and "submission," and some even used phrases such as "One wonders if our British friends are watching a mirage" and "Germany's atrocities are now a beautiful and free gift." Paris now feels that the close cooperation between France and Britain, which has been established recently and has greatly satisfied France, has now been broken. The Paris evening paper declared that France's policy is now swinging between two extremes, one being Moscow and the other being London. If Franco-British cooperation cannot be realized, then Franco-Russian cooperation will naturally follow. (Reuter, 19th)

United States Pays Close Attention 29

(Washington) Secretary of State Hull met here today with President Roosevelt's special envoy Davis, who was specially summoned here, to discuss the European situation. After the meeting, Hull told reporters that the United States is currently adopting a wait-and-see attitude and paying close attention to the situation. Hull and Davis et al. were very concerned after hearing the news of the British note to Germany, but did not wish to express their opinions. Hull said that he had not discussed the European situation with any foreign envoys, nor had he received any official correspondence from foreign governments regarding this matter. The US Ambassador to Germany is constantly reporting all developments in detail to the State Department. Hull and Davis are likely to discuss everything with President Roosevelt in the next few days. Senator Pittman, chairman of the Senate Foreign Relations Committee, told people today that, in his opinion, the United States should not get involved in the European crisis. Germany's decision to rearm is the result of competing countries failing to jointly establish a new defense system except for military alliances. (Reuter, 18th)

(Washington) Regarding Germany's abolition of the military articles of the Treaty of Versailles, Secretary of State Hull did not wish to comment, but the United States now seems to have the following impressions: Germany's decision is enough to eliminate various misunderstandings, the future negotiation situation can be clarified, and the Treaty of Versailles will also suffer a fatal blow as a result. The United States believes that the difficulties that have arisen in Europe after the European War should be blamed in part on Versailles. The US government is now paying attention to studying the impact that European events may have on the Far East, fearing that the Soviet Union will have to increase its western border defenses as a result and neglect its Far East defenses. If so, the United States' position towards Japan will also be weakened as a result. However, this kind of worry is ultimately too vague. What attitude the United States will take towards Germany's actions, and whether it will lodge a protest with Germany when necessary, may not be affected by this kind of concern. (Havas, 18th)

US Fears German-Russian Conflict 30

(Washington) In diplomatic circles here, the intense action of Germany's resumption of conscription is deeply feared to lead to a conflict with Soviet Russia. Although opinions vary, some expect that Soviet Russia will not be able to stand idly by as Hitler, the great enemy of communism, takes on the role of commander of a large army. If a conflict occurs, Poland may side with Germany, and Japan may attack Soviet Russia from the east. Observers say that the Soviet Union currently has an armed force of 830,000 men, and the number of trained reserves is even higher. After the German conscription plan is implemented, it will only have 500,000 men, among whom very few can fight. Senior US Army and Navy officers believe that Germany's action may not lead to war, as this action only restores the balance of power before the war. Moreover, as an important country in Europe, Germany cannot remain excluded from military equipment for long. The US government does not wish to express any formal opinions on this new development in international events, but has held several meetings in recent days, and the State Department was also open all day on Sunday. Government leaders declared that the United States could not have any formal statement before President Roosevelt, Secretary of State Hull, and Special Envoy Davis met at the White House. Davis rushed here from New York on Sunday and had a brief meeting with Hull. (National Telegram, 18th)

(Moscow) Pravda commented on Germany's implementation of universal military service, saying that the significance of this matter is not only the increase in the quantity of German armaments, but the importance of this new step by German imperialism lies in its demonstrative nature. Hitler solemnly declared that the Treaty of Versailles restricted German armaments, so it was just a scrap of paper. This posture towards the Treaty of Versailles was expressed just one week before the British Foreign Secretary's visit to Berlin, and Britain and France were the drafters of the Treaty of Versailles. German fascism has resolutely moved towards war preparations. It opposes the formula of "security first, then disarmament." It does not mention the formula, but takes action directly. Its intention is to say, "Let me arm first, and then talk about peace." The German diplomatic community explains the purpose of its fanatical military expansion with the phrase "Germany wants peace." Pravda commented, "This desire for peace is fully expressed by the German government's inaction on the Eastern European Pact, which is the only tool that truly equally guarantees the security of all signatory countries." Pravda concluded, "It is not superfluous for us to mention at this moment the just observations of the elderly, namely, that the aggression and tactics of the German fascists are based on a belief, namely, that the hesitation and wavering of the policy taken by Britain will at some point enable its tactics to achieve overall victory." Therefore, the phrase "appeal to the German nation" is re-added to the spices of a reply (which is actually extremely vague) to the British Empire. It is not accidental. (TASS, 18th)

Hitler's New Diplomacy 33

(Berlin) The scheduled visit of British Foreign Secretary Simon and Lord Privy Seal Eden to Germany has been confirmed. It is generally believed that the new approach to diplomacy adopted by Führer Hitler can be seen as a victory in this move. Semi-official sources, after the government's decision to restore compulsory military service, were deeply concerned about the global backlash, which is indeed the case, but all are trying to conceal it. This is because the countries concerned, whether in Berlin or Geneva, have not taken joint action, and all are overjoyed. Official circles only vaguely mentioned the British protest, dismissing the British argument that unilateral action should not change treaties as "mere rhetoric," not worth worrying about. The National Socialist Party authorities believe that since equal rights to armaments have been obtained, they only need to intensify negotiations diplomatically. Germany has agreed to participate in the Western European Security Air Pact, but it still seems unable to accept the Eastern European collective security plan. (Havas dispatch on the 19th)

(Berlin) Today, all German national newspapers published an article by Propaganda Minister Goebbels, discussing the reactions of various European countries to Germany's announcement of conscription on March 16. Goebbels stated, "The world's reaction to Germany has caused deep surprise throughout Germany, because Germans firmly believe that the whole world should be reassured and satisfied. Germany's open announcement of the restoration of conscription clearly demonstrates Germany's determination to strive for security and balance of power. For several years, the so-called mystery of Germany's defense problem has provoked several formal and informal protests from the major powers. The most prominent of these protests stated that without a thorough understanding of Germany's intentions, lasting peace is impossible. Since receiving these formal and informal protests, Germany has repeatedly considered abandoning its secret policies and openly declaring its true intentions and the policies it is implementing. The completion of this intention is particularly important today, because newspapers in various countries constantly make empty and unrealistic estimates of Germany's defense capabilities, spreading misinformation and causing mutual panic among nations, which is greatly detrimental to the prospects for peace. Therefore, Mr. Hitler's bold move is sufficient to dispel the above-mentioned rumors and malpractices. On November 28, 1934, during a debate in the British House of Commons, Churchill pointed out that Germany's defense capabilities far exceeded the number of people obtained through the conscription system of March 16. However, Churchill also said at that time, 'Even so, we have no reason to say that the Germans will attack Britain.' Churchill further declared in the same speech that the time had come to dispel the mystery of German armaments. Why, then, does Germany's public declaration of its military strength today provoke such discrimination? Moreover, for the past fifteen years, Germany has hoped that the signatory countries of the Treaty of Versailles would fulfill their disarmament obligations, but instead of disarming themselves, these countries have expanded their armaments. Mr. Hitler has repeatedly declared that if all countries in the world are willing to take the same bold action, Germany would not hesitate to destroy its last gun and bullet, but those who spoke sincerely were ignored. Therefore, today Germany is in a desperate situation and has to face the current facts, knowing that a country without armaments, surrounded by powerful neighbors with great armaments, is sufficient to provoke war. Today, the veil of mystery has been removed, and Germany has emerged to interact with the world's powers on an equal footing. If it can contribute to the guarantee of European peace and the harmony of the world's nations, it is willing to work hard and follow diligently." (National News Agency dispatch on the 18th)

(Berlin) A senior German political figure, in response to an interview with a Havas News Agency reporter, stated that Germany's rearmament has not caused a backlash internationally, which is gratifying. The fact that there has been no international backlash is a victory for Germany. The British note to the German government yesterday has not yet been published. When the Havas News Agency reporter inquired about its content, the senior official said, "The wording of the British note avoids the term 'protest,' and according to its meaning, it does not protest the measures taken by Germany from a legal perspective. In terms of diplomatic language, this note can be said to be appropriate. As for the conditions under which Germany accepted the visit of British cabinet members, the reason is very clear: Germany's position is now much stronger than it was two weeks ago. Since Germany's equal rights to armaments have been obtained, there is no need to discuss this issue further when Britain and Germany hold talks. This is why the German government accepted the visit of British cabinet members." The Havas News Agency reporter further inquired about the number of personnel in Germany's formation of twelve army corps and whether the German navy would also be rearmed, but no definitive answer was given. The conclusion was, "Germany has no territorial demands on France. Hitler has said this repeatedly. Germany hopes to enrich the Locarno Pact, but does not hope for an Eastern European mutual assistance pact, because we already have the German-Polish Treaty, which is sufficient. We hope that Britain can understand this." (Havas dispatch on the 19th)

British House of Commons Passes Army Budget, £450,000 for Anti-Aircraft Guns, Barracks to be Built in Hong Kong to House British Troops 34

(London) The House of Commons discussed the army budget today, which lasted for a long time and repeatedly mentioned Germany's rearmament. Finally, the budget figures were passed. It was found that this figure included £450,000 specifically for improving anti-aircraft guns. The Labour Party moved to reduce the number of army personnel by three thousand, but this motion was defeated in the House of Commons by 206 votes to 44. When Financial Secretary to the War Office Hacking presented this budget, he stated that Germany's decision to rearm made it necessary for Britain to maintain adequate coastal, air, and land defenses. Coastal defenses, whether domestic or foreign, are also being renewed, and there is no sign that the number of British troops overseas can be reduced for the time being. Britain cannot allow the effectiveness of its combat troops' equipment to be inferior to others. The budget provides for a phased approach to ensure that combat troops have the necessary equipment. This is not an expansion of the army, but a slight improvement to reach the appropriate standard that was put aside during the disarmament negotiations. Opposition leader Lansbury requested a debate on the German situation be scheduled before Parliament adjourns. It has now been decided that the debate will be held on Thursday. The date was originally scheduled for the discussion of the India Bill, and the discussion of the India Bill will be postponed at that time. (Reuters dispatch on the 18th)

(London) Financial Secretary to the War Office Cooper answered questions in the House of Commons today regarding the progress of the defense of the British-owned island of Lai, stating that Britain had spent £7,325,000 to build the impregnable naval base in Singapore, and will now allocate another £7,500,000 for the base's military expenses to complete the Far Eastern defense of the British Empire. The small island was a desolate area a hundred years ago, but in the British national defense plan, it has become the Gibraltar of the Far East. A 600-acre aircraft landing strip has now been opened. According to unofficial sources in London, the base is currently increasing its heavy artillery equipment. (National News Agency dispatch on the 19th)

(London) During the debate on the army budget today, the House of Commons mentioned the issue of building barracks in Hong Kong to house three battalions of British troops. Financial Secretary to the War Office Hacking replied that the construction of barracks would have to be done in the future. For now, only £100 is being requested to facilitate the investigation. Specific measures have not yet been determined. If it is necessary, this expenditure will be included in the budget for the following year, at which time the House of Commons will have ample opportunity for discussion. New Soviet Industrial Plan 43

(Moscow) The Soviet People's Committee discussed today the plan for the opening of various new factories this year, the use of which will exceed the planned construction costs for this year, reaching 22,466 million rubles. There are 2,000 large factories currently under construction, of which 1,178 will be fully or partially opened this year. The power generation of power plants will increase by 750,000 kilowatts. In terms of the fuel industry, 41 new coal mines will be added, with a total output of 23.2 million tons. Fourteen new oil crushing plants will be added. New steel plants worth nearly 1.5 billion rubles will be built. The workload of blast furnaces will increase by 10.2%, open-hearth furnaces by 20.8%, rolling mills by 14%, and aluminum plants by 80%. This year, the Soviet Union will have its own magnesium mines. There will be two automobile factories with an output increase of 55,000 vehicles. The opening of new light industry factories will cost 73.8 million rubles, compared to only 48.1 million rubles last year. The new railways that will be open to traffic this year are worth a total of 4.4 billion rubles. The new railways that are regularly open to traffic are 367 kilometers long, and those that are temporarily open to traffic are 1,151 kilometers long. In addition, 3,247 kilometers of double-track railways will be built, of which 2,182 kilometers are in the Far East. New houses worth a total of 2.4 billion rubles will be built. The above is part of the large-scale construction plan of the Soviet Union in 1935. (TASS dispatch on the 18th)

Results of Various Provincial and Municipal Post Offices Selling Revenue Stamps 47

Sales in January Exceeded 780,000 Yuan

(Nanjing) Since the Ministry of Finance transferred the sale of revenue stamps to the post offices, the results have been good, which has greatly benefited the elimination of harsh taxes in various provinces and the income of the national treasury. A Central News Agency reporter learned that the revenue stamps sold by the post offices in November of last year totaled more than 550,000 yuan, which increased to more than 588,000 yuan in December, and increased to more than 780,000 yuan in January. Taking the five provinces of Jiangsu, Fujian, Shandong, Hebei, and Chahar, and the four cities of Beijing, Shanghai, Ping, and Qing as examples, the number of stamps sold in January has exceeded the number sold by the revenue stamp bureaus in each month of the 22nd year of the Republic of China. For example, Shandong Province and Qing City sold more than 74,000 yuan per month in the 22nd year of the Republic of China, but increased to more than 115,000 yuan in January. Hebei Province previously sold more than 86,000 yuan per month, but now increased to more than 143,000 yuan. Ping City previously sold more than 17,000 yuan per month, but now increased to more than 26,000 yuan. Shanghai City and the concessions previously sold more than 78,000 yuan per month, but now increased to more than 114,000 yuan. However, merchants in Zhejiang, Anhui, Jiangxi, and Hubei provinces have failed to affix revenue stamps as required or because of incomplete inspection of the revenue stamps affixed, resulting in the fact that although the number of revenue stamps sold by the post offices in January increased compared to the number sold in November and December of last year, it was still less than the number of stamps sold by the revenue stamp bureaus in each month of the 22nd year of the Republic of China. The number of stamps sold in Anhui, Jiangxi, Hubei, and Henan provinces in January decreased by between 4,900 yuan and 9,900 yuan compared to each month of the 22nd year of the Republic of China, while Zhejiang decreased by as much as 62,000 yuan. In addition to notifying the provincial governments and ordering the provincial and county revenue stamp bureaus to promote inspection, the Ministry of Finance will also send cadres to various places for strict inspection to avoid losses to both the national treasury and the compensation to various provinces. (Central News Agency dispatch on the 19th)

Amendment to the Budget Law to Be Submitted to the Legislative Yuan for Deliberation 57

(Nanjing) Although our country's budget law has been formulated, it has not yet been implemented. However, various agencies have adopted the spirit of the budget law when handling budget proposals. Currently, according to the opinions of budget specialists from the Directorate General of Budgets, Accounts and Statistics, the Ministry of Finance, the National Audit Office, and various agencies in charge of budget proposals, it is generally believed that the budget law, after several years of informal application, urgently needs many amendments. (1) The boundaries stipulated for the budgets of administrative agencies are too strict and should be made more flexible and adaptable. (2) The stipulated period for handling preliminary estimates and budgets is inappropriate and should be adjusted. (3) Various attached tables also need to be improved based on the results of trials and verifications. Based on the above opinions, a certain legislator has compiled them and will soon prepare a bill to be submitted to the Legislative Yuan for deliberation. (19th Central News Agency Dispatch)

Kuancheng Briefly Captured by Volunteer Army 58

(Tianjin) On the 14th, over 500 members of the Volunteer Army were discovered in Kuancheng, a pseudo-Rehe province. They besieged the city. The defending troops consisted of 80 Japanese soldiers and 300 puppet soldiers. After four hours of fierce fighting, the city was captured by the Volunteer Army. On the 15th, the puppet troops gathered a large force for a counterattack. The Volunteer Army, unable to withstand them, retreated ten li east of the city to Qingshengzhuang to await further opportunities. (19th Special Dispatch)

(Beiping) Harness, a student from Princeton University in the United States, came to China for travel. He arrived in Nanjing on Wednesday and departed for Shanghai from Nanjing the next day. Since then, his whereabouts have been unknown. Those concerned have now begun investigating his whereabouts. (19th Reuters Dispatch)

(Nanjing) The Directorate General of Posts has decided to launch a lightweight postal package service starting April 1st and has ordered all post offices nationwide to comply. The weight of each package must not exceed one kilogram, and the minimum postage is 20 cents. Senders can drop the packages into post boxes, and postmen will deliver them to the recipients. (19th Central News Agency Dispatch)

International Commercial Telegrams

—March 19th Reuters Special Business Report— 69

Gold and Silver

British Gold: London gold prices rose again today due to the weakness of the pound, to 147 shillings and 2.5 pence, 3.5 pence higher than yesterday.

British Silver: London silver prices did not rise today due to the fall of the pound. The spot price opened in the afternoon at 27.3125 pence, and the futures price at 27.375 pence, both down 0.0625. The United States and China bought in, India sold out, and China also sold out later.

Exchange Rates

British-American: The foreign exchange market in London this morning was chaotic, with prices fluctuating greatly, but trading was not active. The pound continued to fall. The British-American exchange rate opened at $4.75375, 625 lower than the closing price in the US and UK yesterday. At 11:00, the price rebounded slightly, up 1875, but this rise could not be sustained. At noon, the price was $4.74375, 1.1875 lower than the 11:00 price. Sentiment improved slightly later, so the one o'clock price was $4.74625, but the decline did not stop. At two o'clock, it fell another half a point, with the price at $4.74125.

British-French: The opening price was 71.84 francs, 25 pounds lower than the closing price yesterday. Thereafter, the price remained weak, trending downwards successively. At two o'clock, the price was 71.51 francs, 33 pounds lower than the opening price.

Cotton and Wheat

American Cotton: Before the opening of the market today, Wall Street's attention was focused on the cotton market, as the movement of the cotton market could determine the direction of the New York stock market and the Chicago grain market. The cotton market opened quite actively, with prices 11 points higher than yesterday's closing price. Yesterday's fluctuations have not shaken the stability of the current spot basis price. The current footing is quite firm. Consignment sales to avoid losses without price limits have now been cleared. Short covering has not been discovered. Demand has begun. Within the first hour of opening, market prices continued to advance, rising another 10 to 13 points compared to the opening.

British Cotton: The Liverpool cotton market had a better atmosphere this morning because it was expected that the US cotton market price would definitely rebound after yesterday's decline. The afternoon one o'clock price for May futures was 6.08, up 10 points.

British Wheat: The Liverpool wheat market was also affected because wheat prices in major wheat-producing countries were not stable. Today, the afternoon one o'clock price for May was 4 shillings and 11.75 pence, 25 lower than yesterday's closing price.

Rubber

London: London rubber prices were relatively stable. The transaction prices for July and September futures at noon were 5.625 pence, 15 higher than yesterday's closing price, but the buying momentum was not intense.

New York: New York rubber opened higher, but there was a slight pullback within the first half hour.

Securities

New York: The New York stock market sympathized with the cotton market, and the atmosphere at the opening was better, with prices rising slightly. Trading seemed to be still active. The prices are as follows:

Mei Lanfang Talks About Film to Russian Reporter 104

(Moscow) The "Soviet Art Daily" published an interview with Dr. Mei Lanfang. Mei stated, "I have made a purely theoretical study of excellent dramas in the Soviet Union and Europe, so my coming to the Soviet Union is extremely important for my creative activities. At this moment, I can get close to the stage art and be able to work with theatrical geniuses such as Stanislavski and Meyerhold. It is the first time in my life. I also deeply know that there are many young and promising theatrical groups in the Soviet Union, and they have valuable success." Mei continued, "After my troupe and I perform here several times, we will go to Leningrad and then return to Moscow. After that, Dr. Yu Shangyuan and I will make a tour of Western Europe. The purpose of this troupe's European trip is not for business but purely for cultural and artistic purposes. The reason why I led my troupe to Russia is that its drama is absolutely non-commercial. It is for this reason. After the troupe is familiar with Moscow's artistic life, it will soon return to China." Mei concluded, "I hope that the mutual familiarity between Chinese and Soviet dramas will be able to promote cultural friendship between the Chinese and Soviet people." (18th TASS Dispatch)

The Breach at Changyuan Remains Unblocked, Severe Flooding in Western Shandong 106

Extensive Flooding in Puyang, Fanxian, and Shouyang Counties; Disaster Area Spanning Over 450 Li; Over a Million Starving Disaster Victims

A dispatch from Jinan reports that since the breach at Changyuan on the Yellow River, floodwaters have flowed eastward, entering Shandong Province along the Jin Causeway. Puyang, Fanxian, and Shouyang counties in western Shandong are now submerged. The disaster area stretches over 450 li east to west, from the breach at Changyuan to Taochengbu on the Donghe River in eastern Shandong, before rejoining the main river. No fewer than a million people have been affected. Representatives from Puyang, Fanxian, and Shouyang counties have repeatedly petitioned in Jinan, requesting the closure of the breach. However, as Changyuan is under the jurisdiction of Hebei Province, Shandong Province claims it cannot intervene, resulting in no action. The breach at Guantai continues to widen, increasing the flow of water, and the flooding in western Shandong is worsening. Although the central government has resolved that the National Economic Council, in conjunction with the Ministry of Finance, should discuss relief measures, no concrete decisions have been made. With no hope of spring plowing, hundreds of thousands of disaster victims in western Shandong are starving. They have appointed Jiang Mingqian, Liu Enlun, Zhang Jianling, and Ding Liquan as representatives to telegraph Premier of the Executive Yuan Wang Jingwei and Minister of Finance Kong Xiangxi, urging them to quickly allocate a large sum of money and order the Hebei and Henan provincial governments to close the breach as soon as possible to save the people and protect their lives. Simultaneously, they have telegraphed Shandong Provincial Chairman Han Fuju, requesting him to forward a petition to the central government on behalf of the people. The original telegrams are transcribed below:

Telegram to Ministers Wang and Kong

To Premier Wang of the Executive Yuan and Minister Kong of Finance in Nanjing: The Yellow River has repeatedly breached at Changyuan in recent years, causing severe flooding in Puyang, Fanxian, Shouyang counties of Shandong Province. The breach remains unblocked, and there is no hope for spring plowing. A million lives are at stake. We urgently request a large allocation of funds to order the governments of Hebei, Shandong, and Henan provinces to close the breach immediately and complete the work within a set time limit to save the people and protect their lives. Jiang Mingqian, representative of disaster victims in Shouzhang County, Shandong; Liu Enlun, representative of disaster victims in Yanggu County; Zhang Jianling, representative of disaster victims in Puyang County; Ding Liquan, representative of disaster victims in Fanxian County, respectfully bow.

Telegram to Chairman Han of the Provincial Government

To Chairman Han of the Shandong Provincial Government: Since the Yellow River has repeatedly breached at Changyuan in recent years, the four counties of Shouzhang, Yanggu, Puyang, and Fanxian in Shandong Province have suffered severe flooding. For two years, there have been no harvests, and the livelihood of the farmers has reached its limit. Many young and strong have fled to all directions, while the old and weak await death in their homes. Spring plowing is approaching, but the breach remains unblocked. The water depth in the fields is three to five feet, making it impossible to harvest wheat, and even autumn crops will be difficult to plant on time. Alas, our compatriots are suffering through this calamitous year. The affected area is located south of the Jin Causeway and north of the Linhuang embankment, extending approximately 450 li east to west from Changyuan County in Hebei to Dong'a County in Shandong. Over a million people have been affected. The disaster is undeniably severe, and the affected area is undeniably vast. If no measures are taken to close the breach quickly, the peach blossom floods will soon arrive, and the disaster area will inevitably expand further. In the unfortunate event that the Jin Causeway fails, the Yellow River will shift north, turning Tianjin and other ports into marshlands. The consequences are too terrible to contemplate. As representatives entrusted by hundreds of thousands of disaster victims, we respectfully present the true situation. We respectfully request that you forward this to the Executive Yuan and the Ministry of Finance, urging them to promptly allocate a large sum of money to close the breach as soon as possible to save the people and protect their lives. Apart from sending separate telegrams, we hereby submit this telegram for your review and instruction. Jiang Mingqian, representative of disaster victims in Shouzhang County, Shandong; Liu Enlun, representative of disaster victims in Yanggu County; Zhang Jianling, representative of disaster victims in Puyang County; Ding Liquan, representative of disaster victims in Fanxian County, respectfully bow. (17th)

Hankou City in Hubei Province Issues Construction Bonds 107

Provincial Government Borrows 1.6 Million for Road Construction; City Bonds Used for Construction of City Government and School Buildings

A dispatch from Hankou reports that the Hubei Provincial Government, in order to meet the needs of highway construction, previously obtained central approval to issue 6 million yuan in construction bonds. Provincial Chairman Zhang Qun convened leaders of the Wuhan-Yangxin-Hankou chambers of commerce to discuss fundraising methods. It was decided that the standard for bond purchases would be one month's salary for employees of shops in the three towns of Wuhan, Yangxin, and Hankou, and one month's rent for landlords. The issuance began on April 1st. However, due to the large amount of these bonds, it would be difficult to raise the full amount immediately. During the bandit suppression period, highway construction could not be delayed. In addition to the 600,000 yuan already borrowed from the Bank of Communications and the Hubei Provincial Bank by the Department of Finance to first repair the Hanyi Road, it has now been decided to borrow 1 million yuan against 2 million yuan in bond certificates from the Hankou Banking Syndicate. Negotiations on this matter have been ongoing for days and are nearing completion. Sixteen banks are participating in the loan, including the Bank of China (127,000 yuan), Jin City, Zhongnan, Zhejiang Industrial, Siming, China Agricultural and Industrial, Salt Industry, Continental, Zhejiang Industrial, Shanghai, and China General Commercial banks (63,000 yuan each), China Industrial, China National Products, Juxingcheng, and Guangdong banks (32,000 yuan each), and the Bank of Communications (115,000 yuan). The interest rate is one percent per month, and the loan will be repaid in four installments over thirteen months. The Department of Finance authorities will soon formally sign a contract with the Banking Syndicate leaders. As the provincial construction bonds are about to be issued, the Hankou Municipal Government is also issuing 1.5 million yuan in municipal construction bonds. The uses of these funds have already been determined: 300,000 yuan for the construction of a new municipal government building, 400,000 yuan for the construction of vocational schools and elementary school buildings, and the remaining 800,000 yuan for road construction and the relocation of civilian housing. These bonds have been submitted to the central government for review by the Legislative Yuan and are expected to be issued within two months at the latest. (17th)

Further Report on the Major Prison Break in Songjiang 108

As reported yesterday, a large-scale prison break occurred at this county's prison at 6 PM on the 18th. It is now learned that the prison held a total of 139 inmates. Yesterday afternoon, after the usual lockdown and roll call at 4 PM, the inmates planning the escape took the opportunity to create a disturbance. They broke their shackles and tied up the guards and the warden's family. At that time, Warden Shu Zhang was in the street purchasing food bowls for the inmates and had not yet returned. The police rushed back, and fourteen inmates cut the telephone lines and stormed out of the prison gate, fleeing in different directions towards Wangyun Bridge and other streets. Order in the city was disrupted for a time. Special units of the Public Security Bureau, the water patrol, and the security brigade were dispatched to pursue and capture the escapees. County Magistrate Jin, President Yang, and Chief Prosecutor Zhu all arrived to supervise the situation. They conducted a roll call and ordered strict surveillance. Military police captured two escapees, Zhang Baogen and Lin Yunquan. The remaining twelve escapees are still at large, and search parties are out looking for them. Among the escapees is Xia Ziyun, a local resident serving a life sentence; Xia Damazi and Xia Sanmazi from Yancheng, serving twelve years; Shang Shaorong and Chen Tu, also local residents; Jiang Er from Yancheng; and Hu Musheng, a local resident. All these inmates were convicted of robbery. After the incident last night, patrols around the prison were increased. Today, Warden Li reported the incident to the authorities. County Magistrate Jin and others inspected the prison. The chief guard, surnamed Li, was severely beaten by the escaping inmates. The authorities believe that the chief guard was negligent in his duties and ordered him to be detained for investigation.

Police and Bandits Exchange Fire in Xinta, Suzhou; Rescued Hostage; Two Bandits Killed 109

On the 8th of this month, over twenty bandits from Pudong arrived in Xindong Village, Xinta Township, Wujiang, with intentions to cause trouble. Section Chief Ling of the township dispatched twenty plainclothes police officers, along with Commander Ma of the garrison ship stationed in Luxu, to suppress and capture them. Upon arrival, they encountered the bandits, and both sides opened fire, engaging in a battle for approximately half an hour before the bandits were repelled. Two bandits were killed, Wang Chungeng and Wang Bingchen were captured alive, and a hostage, Zhu Guanguang (from Xitang Township, Zhejiang), was rescued. The hostage has been handed over to Detective Chen Bingkun of Jiaxing to be returned to Zhejiang. Commander Ma reported the incident to the Second District Headquarters yesterday (the 19th) for the record.

County Party Headquarters Stages Drama to Raise Funds for Spring Relief 111

Last year's drought was severe, and suffering was widespread in this county. The County Party Headquarters, recognizing the urgent need for spring relief, is organizing a charitable drama performance, with the local theaters taking turns to perform. The proceeds from ticket sales will be entirely used for spring relief. Yesterday, the performance was held at the Zhongnan Grand Theater, with actors from the Pingju Xin Guang and Qingsheng theaters, and special appearances by the son of the famous performer Xiao Dazi, Li Shaochun, and all the talented actors from the Xiu Ji Gengxin theater. It was a grand occasion.

Armed Conflict Erupts Again in the Shatian Case in Changshu 112

The Fulidi and Dingfeng companies in Shazhou City have repeatedly engaged in armed conflicts over the issue of constructing Shatians, disregarding human lives. Recently, the Department of Finance ruled that the county-administered township concession should demarcate the two companies to separate them, and that they should no longer dispute. Secretary Li of the County Government went to the township to establish this agreement. Recently, Jin Minjun from the County Shatian Bureau, Qian Zhun from the County Government, and Wu Zongbao from the Department of Finance were dispatched to jointly monitor the demarcation. All the commissioners arrived in the township the other day, but found that the previously agreed boundary had been uprooted by the Fulidi Company, which had redrawn it more than a hundred zhang into Dingfeng's land. Dingfeng was extremely dissatisfied and was about to inquire when another dispute erupted. Hundreds of sand farmers from each side gathered, resulting in Chen Shengjie of Dingfeng being severely injured. The commissioners were also obstructed and had to retreat, awaiting a resolution of the dispute before returning to the township. Both sides have sent the injured to the city for medical treatment and have reported the incident to the County Bureau. As a result, this year-long dispute over the Shatians remains unresolved.

Zhenjiang: Jiangsu Farmers Bank Opens; Loans for Seedlings and Silkworm Cocoons Granted 113

The Jiangsu Provincial Farmers' Bank has been effective in assisting rural development in the past. With spring plowing now underway, all spring loans have been opened. Loans for seedlings and silkworm rearing in particular will greatly benefit agricultural production. The methods are described as follows: (1) Seedling loans are provided in the spring and summer, limited to purchasing fertilizer, seeds, agricultural tools, livestock, and machine oil. Farmers applying for loans must detail the number of mu cultivated, the types of crops, and the intended use of the funds. After approval by the bank, loans are issued in kind to prevent misuse. The loan amount is approximately 50% of the expected harvest, and the harvest is designated as collateral. Since the establishment of agricultural product distribution centers in Shanghai and other locations, purchasing seeds, fertilizer, and agricultural tools has become more convenient. Farmers can substitute in-kind collateral for loan applications. This year, the total loan amount has been increased to 4 million yuan to ensure widespread coverage. (2) Silkworm rearing loans are provided twice a year, in spring and autumn. Farmers rearing silkworms can apply for loans, limited to purchasing silkworm eggs and mulberry leaves. Those purchasing eggs will be provided with improved breeds by the bank, and the sericulture guidance center will send personnel to provide guidance. These loans are most common in Wuxi, Wujiang, Suzhou, and other areas. In recent years, silk prices have plummeted, and banks have seen little profit. Few cocoon markets have opened, and silkworm farmers lack outlets for their fresh cocoons, which is a major issue. The bank cannot establish its own cocoon markets to purchase cocoons, so it has implemented a regulation allowing loans to cocoon markets to enable timely openings and avoid affecting the sale of fresh cocoons.

Ningbo: Major Fire in Nanjia Village, Yin County 114

Wang Yunzhang, a resident of Huaiqing Bridge in Nanjia Village, a carpenter with some savings, bought two houses last month. As they were still being repaired, he was temporarily residing in the empty house of Wang Shanzai. At approximately 5 PM last night, a fire broke out in that house. The fire was extremely fierce and impossible to approach. Fortunately, the fire brigade arrived and extinguished the flames after a period of time. After investigation, it was found that over twenty houses, including those of Wang Renren, Wang Shanhua, and Wang Heshang, and six single-story houses were destroyed. Wang Yunzhang's newly purchased houses were spared due to the efforts of the firefighters. The total loss in the village is estimated at around 10,000 yuan.

Local News

Ministry of Finance Orders Bank of China to Devise Methods for Relief of Industry and Commerce 115

Compilation of News from Various Sources

New Sound News Agency reports that regarding the plan to relieve industry and commerce, the Ministry of Finance has ordered the Bank of China to devise suitable methods. Local associations and the Municipal Chamber of Commerce have also issued statements. A compilation is provided below:

Ministry of Finance Orders Bank of China

Emergency Plan for Relief of Industry and Commerce: (1) Small Credit Loans; (2) Commodity Mortgage Loans. The Association requested the Minister of Finance, Kong, to adopt and implement these plans. The Ministry replied: "Received. The current state of industry and commerce necessitates relief. The emergency relief plans, which you state should be organized and implemented by the Bank of China-led syndicate, should be carefully considered and reported back. Please be informed."

Reply from the Municipal Chamber of Commerce

The Shanghai Municipal Chamber of Commerce replied: "In response to your letter and the attached two emergency plans for relieving industry and commerce, we acknowledge your concern. The Chamber has long been deliberating on methods to revive the market. Previously, we agreed on five measures with the Local Association (already reported). We have separately submitted letters to the Ministry of Finance, the Central Bank, the Savings Guarantee Reserve Committee, and the banking and money trade associations for adoption and implementation. Your letter is appreciated. However, the second measure, Commodity Valuation and Mortgage Loans, corresponds to the fifth measure proposed by us. We have already requested the Central Bank, the Bank of Communications, and the Bank of China to accept these mortgages as much as possible. The first measure, Small Industrial and Commercial Credit Loans, is also consistent with the fourth measure proposed by us. If the government promotes these relief measures and the banking and money trades support them, they will be mutually beneficial and effective. We have discussed and agreed on the outlines of four key points for small industrial and commercial credit loans with the Local Association and have submitted them to the Ministry of Finance for adoption and implementation today. We are replying accordingly for your information."

Letter from the Local Association

The Shanghai Local Association replied: "In response to your letter proposing two relief plans for the urgently needed relief of industry and commerce in this port, we convened a special committee meeting on the 9th to discuss the first plan, Small Industrial and Commercial Credit Loans. We propose that the Bank of China and the money trade launch a syndicate with a total of 5 million yuan to provide small loans specifically for industry and commerce. At the same time, the Municipal Chamber of Commerce and the Local Association will request the Ministry of Finance to allocate funds. The procedures for the loans will be determined by the syndicate. We await the separate decisions and implementation by the Municipal Chamber of Commerce, the Banking Association, and the Money Trade Association. We are replying accordingly for your information."

Separate Letters to Various Groups

After receiving replies from the Municipal Chamber of Commerce and the Local Association, industry and commerce are preparing to first conduct surveys and registrations to accurately determine the need for small credit loans. The original letter stated: "We have learned that the Local Association and the Municipal Chamber of Commerce have discussed and replied regarding the two emergency relief plans for industry and commerce agreed upon by our conference. We are enclosing the replies. If any of your members require these loans, please conduct surveys and registrations for preparation. Once the implementation date is set, or if difficulties arise along the way, our conference will still be responsible for lobbying the relevant groups." At the same time, a pledge form is being drafted to invite various groups to participate in the organization to facilitate progress.

Bankers' Luncheon

Members of the Banking Association, such as Zhang Gongquan, Tang Shoumin, Xu Jiyu, Ye Fuxiao, Bei Songsun, and others, over ten in total, had lunch at the Banking Association conference room at noon yesterday, adjourning at around 1 PM. A New Sound News Agency reporter learned that the association holds a luncheon every Tuesday, where they discuss various issues. Yesterday's luncheon touched on small industrial and commercial credit loans, but no decisions were made.

Subcommittee Discussion

Regarding the proposal for 5 million yuan in small industrial and commercial credit loans, the Local Association and others decided that the government and the money trade would each provide half of the funds. Although the money trade has decided not to join the syndicate, the government and the banks will continue to implement the plan. The members of the subcommittee formed by the Banking Association are Chen Guangfu, Tang Shoumin, Xu Jiyu, Ye Fuxiao, Bei Songsun, and Wang Yansong. It has now been decided that Chen Guangfu will convene a meeting to discuss how to jointly implement the plan for small industrial and commercial credit loans with the government as soon as he returns to Shanghai today.

Wang Yansong's Remarks

Yesterday, a New Sound News Agency reporter interviewed Wang Yansong, a consultant to the Municipal Chamber of Commerce, at the Silk Industry Bank, seeking his opinion on the issue of market recovery. Mr. Wang delivered the following remarks: "The current economic downturn in Shanghai is complex. The bankruptcy of rural areas, the massive trade deficit, the outflow of silver, and the ripple effects of the global economic crisis are all major factors. In simple terms, it is deeply affected by the decline of the entire national economy. Therefore, from the government to the common people, everyone is in a difficult situation, with little disparity in hardship and happiness. Whether we can overcome the difficulties and return to prosperity depends on whether we can focus on self-awareness and self-help, one heart and one mind. In this situation, if all sectors of the country blame each other or make overly high demands without considering reality, it will not help and will only increase the terror. As the saying goes, 'Adversity builds a nation.' We should not be discouraged by this. First, we must stabilize people's minds, and then, with a calm attitude and a hardworking spirit, from the government to the financial, industrial, and commercial sectors and the general public, we must work together with one heart and one mind to reduce the huge trade deficit, balance international payments, and prevent the further outflow of silver. This is the fundamental solution. The short-term measures proposed by the Municipal Chamber of Commerce and others are generally appropriate, but in my opinion, they still require the genuine cooperation of all parties. The commercial acceptance bill created by the silk industry is a way to increase the circulation of capital and allow stagnant accounts between companies to become more flexible. It is a way for each industry to save itself with its own strength. If each industry can work hard separately and cooperate fully, the current impasse may be gradually broken."

The Money Trade Has Replied

The Money Trade Association decided that the business of money houses is primarily based on credit loans, and there is no need to join the syndicate. At the same time, Chairman Qin Runqing urged member money houses to undertake as much business as possible. The Association has now replied to the Local Association with the resolutions of the extraordinary general meeting of members. According to a New Sound News Agency reporter, there are a total of 57 member money houses in the Money Trade Association. If each house can expand its industrial and commercial credit loans by an average of 50,000 yuan, it would increase the financial assistance to industry and commerce by 2.85 million yuan.

Real Estate Developers Plan to Issue Circulating Notes; Banking Circles Denounce as a Wild Scheme; Absolutely Impossible to Realize 116

Central News Agency reports that real estate developer Cheng Linsheng and others recently held a meeting to discuss ways to revive the market and resolved to organize the Shanghai Commercial and Economic Association to prepare for the issuance of 50 million yuan in real estate circulating notes. Yesterday morning, a Central News Agency reporter inquired with banking circles about their opinions on this matter. Most banking leaders denounced this as a wild scheme and stated that it could not be realized under any circumstances. They explained the main reasons why it could not be realized: "A group of real estate developers wants to raise 50 million yuan in real estate circulating notes to relieve the economic downturn, which is commendable. But how can these 50 million yuan in circulating notes be issued? And once issued, how can they circulate in the market? This is a major question. According to the association's proposal, the circulating notes would be like paper money, so the issuance of 50 million yuan in circulating notes would require a 60% cash reserve. In other words, issuing 50 million yuan in real estate circulating notes would require 30 million yuan in cash reserve. The total amount of silver in Shanghai is only 300 million yuan, so it would be very difficult for a group of real estate developers to raise this 30 million yuan cash reserve. Furthermore, the real estate developers are acting unilaterally in proposing the issuance of circulating notes. If they were to issue them, would they be understood and exchanged by all parties? All these are major questions. Therefore, we have no other opinion on this move by the real estate developers except to see it as a wild scheme. It is absolutely impossible to realize."

According to the opinion of the Banking Association, even if this plan achieves 1% success, it would only benefit a small number of real estate developers by turning their real estate into liquid assets. While this would be a great benefit to them, allowing them to adjust and maneuver, it would not have any beneficial impact on society as a whole. The Banking Association believes in a steady approach to market recovery and rejects unrealistic schemes.

According to the Zhonglian News Agency, three veterans, Li Shihui, Wu Zhihui, and Zhang Jingjiang, due to receiving an invitation from Chairman Chiang in Chongqing to enter Sichuan, boarded the Minsheng Company's Yongnian steamboat the night before last at 12:00 AM, heading west into Sichuan. Shenxin No. 7 Factory Decides to Redeem - Principles Agreed Upon, Efforts Made to Raise Large Sum - Chen Guangfu Goes to Beijing for Instructions, Will Return to Shanghai 121

According to the Xinsheng News Agency, after the Shenxin Textile No. 7 Factory was auctioned by the British-owned HSBC Bank, Mayor Wu and others negotiated with the bank for redemption and have already reached an agreement. Efforts are now being made to raise funds. Details are as follows:

Redemption Principles Agreed Upon: Lawyer Okamoto, a Japanese national who bid at the limited price of 2.25 million, insisted on not disclosing the buyer's name, making it impossible to know it until now. Whether the payment has been made is also questionable. However, according to the Xinsheng News Agency reporter's investigation, whether the payment has been made or not is not of great significance. After Mayor Wu and others negotiated with the head of HSBC Bank, it has now been decided in principle to redeem. However, raising the large sum of 2.25 million yuan is the most important key at present.

Chen Guangfu Goes to Beijing to Discuss Fundraising: Rong Zongjing, the general manager of Shenxin Textile Company, believes that it is impossible to raise funds for the 2.25 million yuan redemption during this time of extreme economic difficulty, and the only hope is the government. Now, the second person in charge, Chen Guangfu, the general manager of Shanghai Bank, has gone to Beijing to seek instructions from the Executive Yuan, the Ministry of Industry, and the Ministry of Finance. He is scheduled to return to Shanghai today or tomorrow. Whether the redemption funds will be borne by the government or arranged by Chinese merchant banks will depend on the outcome of Chen's negotiations with the government.

Shenxin No. 7 Continues to Operate as Usual: The Shenxin No. 7 Factory on Yangshupu Road has 56,284 yarn spindles, 13,440 thread spindles, 449 looms, and about 4,000 workers. It continues to operate as usual, and has not yet received a handover notice from the British-owned HSBC Bank. The reason is that after Mayor Wu and others negotiated, a redemption agreement has been reached. Therefore, HSBC Bank is waiting for our side to prepare the funds for redemption. Once the funds are raised, it will be implemented. In short, the redemption is no longer a problem.

Art Exhibition Preview - Antiquities to be Displayed Soon 122

According to the Central News Agency, the London Chinese Art Exhibition has been in preparation for two months. The review and selection of antiquities, except for porcelain, bronzes, jade, silk tapestries, and cloisonné, is complete. Municipal Party Headquarters Notice - Production and Issuance of Badge Styles and Methods - All People's Organizations Should Strictly Comply 125

The Municipal Party Headquarters of this city received a notice from the Central People's Movement Guidance Committee regarding the methods for various agencies, organizations, and shops to produce badges, and issued a notice to all people's organizations in the city yesterday to comply. The notice and methods are recorded below:

Party Headquarters Notice: For notification matters, according to the Central People's Movement Guidance Committee Notice No. 9436, it states that "according to the Jiangsu Provincial Executive Committee's report, 'The Rugao County Executive Committee requests instructions on stipulating the style of badges for people's organizations,' etc. Regarding the style of badges for people's organizations, the National Government convened a badge method discussion meeting with the capital security agencies in January of the 20th year, which resulted in a resolution. However, that method was limited to the capital. Now, upon approval of the committee's request for instructions, it should be handled according to the second item of the resolution of the badge method discussion meeting regarding people's organizations, but the color drawing must first be submitted to the local party headquarters and the competent authorities for record before it can be cast. In addition to replying to the Jiangsu Executive Committee, a copy of the badge method discussion meeting resolution is enclosed for notification and to inform all subordinates, etc." A copy of the badge method discussion meeting resolution is attached to the notice. It is hereby recorded in the newspaper for notification, and all people's organizations in the city should comply, etc. This is a special notice.

Badge Method: "Badge Method Discussion Meeting Resolution," (1) All agencies under the Party, government, and military should uniformly use a circular badge with a diameter of 3 centimeters. (2) People's organizations should use a horizontal rectangle 5 centimeters long and 2 centimeters wide. Educational organizations should use an equilateral triangle 3 centimeters on a side. Shops and other organizations, if badges are necessary, may use a shield shape 6.5 centimeters long and 4 centimeters wide, but can only sign and print the store name and number. (3) The material and color of each badge should be drawn by each agency themselves. (4) The badges of Party, government, and military agencies can be produced by the printing bureau to prevent fraud. The badges of people's and other organizations should first submit color pattern drawings to the police department for record and then be manufactured by a badge shop. (5) Those who wear badges can only wear the badge of their own agency. If going to another agency for business, they can wear the badge of the agency they are visiting at the same time, but must store the badge after the matter is over. (6) No badges of any kind may be worn to entertainment venues, theaters, bookstores, amusement parks, etc. (7) After stipulating the badges of each agency, it must be submitted to the National Government to order the Capital Garrison Headquarters and the Capital Police Department to crack down on them at any time according to the case to show solemnity.

The Municipal Government received an order from the Executive Yuan yesterday, stating, "Ancha previously reported by the Central Antiquities Preservation Committee, based on a report from the Fujian Minhou County Scenic Spots and Antiquities Preservation Association, that this association was organized in accordance with the Ministry of Interior's promulgated regulations on the preservation of scenic spots and antiquities. Now, Article 17 of the Implementing Rules for the Antiquities Preservation Law also stipulates the existence of an Antiquities Preservation Committee. All local antiquities preservation organs, except those directly under the Central Antiquities Preservation Committee, all other such organs in various places should immediately stop activities in accordance with the last year's telegrams co-signed by President Wang and Chairman Chiang, and await the Central Antiquities Preservation Committee's overall planning for reorganization or abolition, and please the Executive Yuan to order the provincial and municipal governments to comply,' etc., which was submitted and passed at the 198th meeting of this court. Carelessness at Jinliyuan Wharf No. 14 Warehouse Last Night 142

At 9:10 last night, a fire broke out suddenly at Jinliyuan China Merchants Bureau No. 14 warehouse (located at the corner of Taiwan Road), No. 47 on the Bund of the French Concession. Nearby patrol officers discovered it and urgently reported to the police station to report to the fire department, which dispatched fire trucks to the rescue. At that time, the wind was very strong, the flames were soaring, and the fire was illuminating the sky. The firefighters all bravely rescued, but the warehouse was full of paper materials, and the downstairs was full of tung oil, all of which were flammable materials. Therefore, the fire continued to increase even after 11:30 p.m. Because the warehouse was surrounded by high walls, the fire broke through the roof, with very small portions of the flames, making the shooting difficult. All insurance companies sent personnel to investigate. The exact amount of loss is not yet estimated. The French Police Department specially sent Chinese and foreign detectives to take care of the scene. The trams on all routes to the 16th Pier were diverted when they reached the Xin Kai He Bund station. The cause of the fire is not easy to determine for a while. However, according to nearby merchants and neighbors, the Jinliyuan warehouse has a total of 20 new and old warehouses, and this is the 14th old warehouse, which has a history of more than 70 years. The warehouse originally belonged to Qichang Warehouse, and later transferred to China Merchants Bureau. In the past year, there have been rumors of reconstruction, but it has been delayed until now and no construction has been seen. The goods usually stored in the warehouse are mainly tung oil, paper, and medicinal materials. No one lives in the warehouse to watch it, and the goods are locked tightly after they are stored. Moreover, smoking is absolutely prohibited during the working hours of porters. Now it is suddenly burned, which is completely unexpected.

Wu Xingya Instructs Students of Labor Movement, Saving the Nation Requires Labor-Capital Coordination, So As to Restore National Capital with Strength, Belief in Doctrine Should Penetrate General Manager's Proposition 143

The Labor Movement Personnel Training Institute established by the Municipal Party Department of this city has been developing rapidly since its establishment. Daily life is very tense. Military management is implemented in the institute, and meals, accommodation, and internal affairs are all thoroughly militarized. Although the work is extremely heavy, the design of teaching and training is meticulous in all aspects, and the students' spirit is not boring or tired. Wu Xingya, the director, and Zhu Xuefan, the deputy director, are able to carry out all matters in the institute responsibly in accordance with the policies shown by the Municipal Party Department. Mr. Wu delivered a speech to all the labor movement personnel yesterday morning. The following is a record of his speech: (1) Regarding the principles of today's labor movement, Mr. Wu pointed out in detail the stages of the Kuomintang's labor policy in the past 15 years. He regretted that since the completion of the Northern Expedition, although the party has carried out the purification of the party and removed tangible communists, the toxins of intangible communism and theories still remain because the party has not yet sorted out its own theories to make them systematic and detailed, and because of the position of the workers themselves. Those who are ignorant of the facts and cling to abstract theories mistakenly believe that class struggle is the justice of labor movement theory. This is a very serious mistake and a very dangerous root cause. Regardless of whether the world revolution is still a fantasy today, and even if it is possible, the path to success cannot be the same everywhere. China has China's national conditions and environment. From a positive perspective, China today is in the stage of developing national capital. State-owned industries are necessary, but supporting private capital is also a strategy that should be adopted today. Today, China takes saving the poor and saving poverty as the primary task, and it is necessary to produce more and consume less, separate construction, and not destroy. It is even more necessary to combine the strength of the people of the whole country and the strength of the entire nation to seek success in things that are not successful. Dividing the strength of the people of the country and destroying the national united front is to hinder the strength of the country and hinder the restoration of the nation, and undoubtedly commits a major crime. Under the above premise, a policy of labor-capital coordination is naturally generated, and the correctness and rationality of the labor-capital coordination policy should naturally be recognized. However, in the process of national capital development, in order to prevent the abuses of communism, we must use the strongest political power and the strongest political power of partyization to gradually expand the power of state-owned industries and limit the power of private capital, so as not to violate the teachings of the General Manager and not violate the principles of the Three People's Principles. (2) Regarding personal cultivation, Mr. Wu earnestly warned the students that they must encourage themselves with the eight words "hard work, hard work, effort, and struggle", and pointed out that cultivation is not only in the passive personal aspect, but also in the active career aspect. The task of labor movement personnel is to seek welfare for the workers and to promote the progress of the country and society based on the party's doctrine and policies. Then, all matters that are beneficial to the workers, such as labor hygiene, labor education, cooperative undertakings, etc., must represent the demands of the workers and carry out reasonable propositions. Otherwise, it is to abandon the post, disloyal to the post, that is, a lack of virtue in cultivation. (Da Gong News Agency)

If citizens are careless, they will get sick, especially because all diseases break out in spring. At this time, citizens should wear more clothes to avoid being invaded by illness.
