Supplement of the Local Edition of Shen Bao

Talks

Confucius Revisits the New World 234

— Chunyu

Jinan telegram of the 13th: According to Japanese Consul Nishida, the new Confucius Temple built by the Yushima Confucian Society in Tokyo, Japan, is scheduled to hold its completion ceremony on April 28th, and will expand the Confucius memorial ceremony. At that time, prominent scholars and celebrities from inside and outside the region will be invited to participate. Since this province is Confucius' hometown (whether the so-called hometown refers to Shandong), special attention will be paid. It is planned to invite one descendant each from the Yan, Zeng, Si, and Meng families, as well as two famous Confucian scholars from the local area, to participate, and travel expenses will be given. If direct descendants do not go, they can send representatives.

When I read this news, I laughed. If Lu Province is Confucius' hometown, then Yushima is his adopted hometown. Although Confucius traveled around the countries and was busy on the road, going everywhere, he had never been to Japan. Now he is making a trip to the Eastern Sea, which is much more glorious than Mei Lanfang and Hu Die going to Moscow to perform and visit the movies. In the future, if anyone wants to invite him, the old man may be happy to go. Isn't this Confucius revisiting the New World?

But Confucius's doctrine is to respect the Zhou Dynasty, resist the barbarians, advocate benevolence and righteousness, and reject hegemonic tactics. Therefore, when he wrote the Spring and Autumn Annals, he wrote what should be written and cut what should be cut, without any mercy. Therefore, Confucius wrote the Spring and Autumn Annals, and rebellious ministers and traitors were afraid. I wonder if Confucius is willing or not to go to Japan this time? Moreover, Confucius was born in Lu, grew up in Lu, and died in Lu. His family lived in Shandong for generations and never moved from their old home. Now Japan wants to invite him to move to Yushima to live, to change and change fresh air. I am afraid that Confucius is attached to his homeland and will not necessarily think about floating on the sea on a raft again, right?

Although Confucius is known as a sage, he was unusually stubborn by nature. Therefore, Confucius traveled in a carriage with two horses, and if he disagreed with someone, he would leave. Moreover, he was most afraid and opposed to fighting. In the past, knives, spears, and halberds already felt cruel, not to mention airplanes and cannons now. Duke Ling of Wei asked Confucius about military formations, and Confucius replied: "I have heard of sacrificial vessels, but I have not studied military affairs." He left the next day. On another occasion, Confucius was also in Wei, and it happened that Kong Wenzi of Wei was about to attack Taishu and asked Zhongni for advice. Zhongni said, "I don't understand." He turned around, took his luggage, and left, saying, "Birds choose trees, but how can trees choose birds?" Therefore, Confucius was extremely opposed to the imperialists' policy of aggression.

Moreover, Confucius also had a problem, that is, he was not persistent. Confucius traveled around the countries for decades, and the longest he stayed was only three or four years, and the shortest was only a few months, before he had to go. Even if Japan invites him to the Eastern Sea this time, Confucius will definitely not stay long. Not only are the principles incompatible, but he also has a very deep sense of homeland. As soon as he encountered matters of war, he would run back home. Therefore, when Confucius was in Chen, Chen was once attacked by bandits. Confucius said, "Let's go back, let's go back. The young men of my party are wild and uninhibited, yet they are accomplished in literature. They are progressive and do not forget their beginnings, but I do not know how to restrain them." He was unwilling to be an official in a foreign country, and was willing to return to his hometown and be an old gentleman of scholarship. It can be seen that his sense of homeland is deep.

Or it may be said that Confucius dared to live among the Nine Yi because the air in the State of Lu was not good, or that it was humble. He firmly said, "If a gentleman lives there, what humility is there?" Therefore, Zhu Xi commented, "Where a gentleman lives, it will be transformed, what humility is there?" It can be seen that Confucius has also never thought of traveling abroad to promote his governing principles with the teachings of benevolence and righteousness. Therefore, he said, "I have heard of those who transform the Chinese into barbarians, but I have not heard of those who transform into barbarians." He was determined to use the principle of persuasion to transform other ethnic groups. Confucius's original goal was like this, so Confucius has also never denied the possibility of moving.

But although Confucius traveled around the countries, he could go everywhere. If he could transform them well, he would stay for a few more days. If he could not transform them well, he would leave. Therefore, he was determined not to move his home, saving a lot of trouble. Therefore, Confucius sometimes looks like an honest man, sometimes like a fool, but sometimes he is also very slippery and opportunistic. Confucius lived in Chen for three years, and it happened that Jin and Chu were competing to be strong, and they attacked Chen. Confucius then left. When he passed through Pu, he happened to encounter Gongshushi rebelling with Pu. The people of Pu detained Confucius, saying to Confucius, "If you do not go to Wei, we will let you go." Confucius made an oath with them, and then let Confucius out from the east gate. Confucius then went to Wei. Zigong said, "Can an oath be broken?" Confucius said, "It was a coerced oath, the gods will not listen, damn him." Now that Japan is preparing for war, it can be seen that Confucius will not necessarily go to Japan.

Therefore, I know that if Japan wants to invite Confucius to travel, Confucius will politely decline, saying, "I am very grateful for your kindness, but the old man is old, I am not accustomed to the water and soil here, I dare not accept your order." Afterwards, he will definitely take the zither and play it, saying, "Heaven is about to destroy culture, and those who die later will not be able to participate in culture. If Heaven does not destroy culture, what can the people of Kuang do to me."

Filial Daughter Temple 235

— Hu Weixiong

Since the beginning of spring, the weather has been exceptionally good. Every day I explore secluded spots and search for scenic beauty, an extravagance that doesn't seem fitting for someone who is ill. Having been here for less than two months, when I look in the mirror, my cheeks appear much fuller, and my spirits are indescribably lifted: this is naturally thanks to my friend. Last week, I sent him a lengthy letter of several thousand words, and because I didn't reread it, his reply indicated that he hadn't initially hoped I, a young person, would become so world-weary. Actually, I dare not entertain such thoughts, but being so attached to this idyllic paradise, I can't help but be emotionally moved. After reading his letter, I couldn't be bothered to explain myself. My vacation is also coming to an end, and the whip of life is already raised high. Can survival really be resolved through "world-weariness"? Cherishing this remaining time, I continue to banish myself to secluded environments each day.

Within the surrounding villages, my footprints are everywhere. One day, I casually mentioned wanting to venture a little further afield. The old lady told me that ten li away, there is a temple called Filial Daughter Temple. Legend has it that it was founded by the daughter of a certain Song Dynasty prime minister who, after her father's death, shaved her head here. However, later it was inhabited by monks and called a temple. Even the abbot, who propagates this story, doesn't know its origin. Since then, every year in the first month, village girls and women who aspire to be filial daughters travel from afar to burn incense and kowtow four times. The lively scene far surpasses any temple fair.

I don't usually like to join in the crowds, but experiencing such a unique custom once couldn't hurt. It was already the end of the month, and the host hired a small boat for me, as the only way to reach the Filial Daughter Temple is by water. The seven-year-old child naturally became my companion again.

The small boat traveled along the same river where we were prevented from walking in the snow that day. After turning a bend, a new world unfolded before my eyes. I couldn't estimate the size of the cemetery of unknown families. Towering pines and cypresses lined a solemn path to the tombs. It's a pity that my little friend can't recount the journey, which is regrettable. However, today's purpose is to see the spectacle at the Filial Daughter Temple, so I shouldn't ask for too much.

After about two hours on the water, we reached the Filial Daughter Temple. Even when we could only glimpse the red walls from afar, we could already hear the sounds of gongs and cymbals. The banks were lined with neatly dressed farm women, an endless stream. Our small boat docked in front of the temple, and a group of children gathered around, but they retreated in disappointment when they saw three men jump out of the boat. In front of the temple was a large open space, filled with various food vendors. The filial daughters, not afraid of losing face, crowded around the snack stalls to fill their stomachs. It's no exaggeration to say that we spent a great deal of effort getting from the riverbank to the temple gate. Today, this place was like a martial arts arena. Only if you had great strength could you get ahead. Trying to politely say hello was a waste of time. No one would pay you any attention.

The Filial Daughter Temple appeared quite grand. Because I didn't dare compete with the filial daughters, I, like others, simply watched the spectacle. After admiring a statue of a figure that was neither clearly male nor female in the main hall, I retreated. According to the boatman, the temple has five courtyards. Behind the hall is a large vegetable garden, and the main hall is in the third courtyard, so one can only superficially estimate the grandeur of the Filial Daughter Temple.

In the second courtyard, a dozen well-fed monks were chanting scriptures loudly, putting on a pious display. None of them dared to steal a glance from the corner of their eyes at the numerous filial daughters before them. If it weren't for the boatman's explanation on the way back, I would have been deceived.

It turns out that the temple's expenses are entirely reliant on the incense offerings from the first month. Two eloquent reception monks specialize in soliciting donations from the more affluent filial daughters by presenting donation registers. So, regardless of their misdeeds during ordinary times, they put on a serious facade and perform Buddhist rituals today as a means of collecting money. As a result, I became somewhat skeptical of the legend of the filial daughter. Unexpectedly, in this tranquil environment, as I was about to depart, I was given such a disappointing impression.

A Family of Three 236

— Lini

Just as the sky outside the glass window began to brighten, Xiao Lin tumbled out of bed, humming a tuneless song like a little sparrow. She stretched out her small hand, stroking Lin's fluffy hair, then turned around and pried open my eyelids, shaking my body and buzzing around my ears like a fly.

"Daddy, I want to buy a 'doo-doo' car... a 'doo-doo' car!"

Yesterday, Xiao Lin saw the new "doo-doo" car that the landlord's son had bought, which greatly pleased her childish heart. She secretly ran downstairs and played with her little friend in the living room, so much so that she didn't even want to come up for dinner. It wasn't until Lin went down to pick her up that she reluctantly came upstairs, still refusing to eat properly, crying and demanding to buy a "doo-doo" car.

"Okay, don't make a fuss. After you finish eating, Daddy will go to the company tomorrow and buy you a 'doo-doo' car. Be good!"

The little child's mind seemed to be still thinking about her beloved toy. She slept restlessly at night, muttering in her dreams and clamoring for a "doo-doo" car.

"Don't make a fuss. It's still early. Wait a bit and Daddy will go out and buy it for you."

Then, the little child happily smiled innocently, then slipped out of bed, humming a tuneless song, and ran downstairs to find her little friend to play with. Lin saw the child's innocent and happy expression and gave me an understanding smile.

A child's liveliness, innocence, pure and unadulterated expressions, and laughter can indeed fill a small family with joy and liveliness. However, sometimes, because of the child's affairs, the parents' minds are filled with anxiety and worry.

Sometimes, if the child catches a cold, her body feels uncomfortable, her smiling face is tightly shut, and she lies listlessly on the bed, dazed and losing her original innocence. She doesn't want to eat or talk. At this time, Lin doesn't know whether to laugh or cry, hiding in the room all day long, frowning and holding the child tightly in her arms, sighing and rocking her. She doesn't even have the heart to do housework. At this time, the air in the room feels particularly dull and depressing. Even the relationship between husband and wife feels cold, like two strangers who happen to meet and are indifferent to each other.

"Ren, I think we should buy Xiao Lin a 'doo-doo' car," Lin said hesitantly, while her heart seemed to feel a kind of extreme happiness. "Otherwise, when she sees other people's 'doo-doo' cars, she will cry and make a fuss... Wouldn't it be worse if she makes herself sick?"

I know that Lin cherishes her child the most.

Page 19

She will try her best to grant whatever the child wants. She would rather save as much as possible on household expenses than let the child feel the pain of disappointment, so as not to hurt her childish heart.

"How can we afford it? A 'doo-doo' car costs at least ten dollars! ... The child will naturally forget about it completely in a day or two."

I thought about how difficult it is to earn a dozen dollars and our current economic situation. Buying a "doo-doo" car for the child to play with seems a bit unsuitable for our status. However, Xiao Lin suddenly ran upstairs again, standing in front of the bed like a little sparrow, buzzing around me and wanting to buy a "doo-doo" car.

At this time, I deeply felt that this small family of three has become a bit too heavy to bear.

After Abandonment 237

— Jingyun

The spring breeze, carrying a warm breath, leaked through the continuous, overlapping mountains of Meiling, awakening the two car-cover-like locust trees in front of Uncle Siwei's black gate, adorning them with a suit of tender green clothes, and swaying proudly in the warm spring breeze. The people in the village, bathed in the warm spring breeze, presented an air of new life and vitality, busily carrying seedlings and heading to the fields to work.

At this time, the two black-lacquered doors of Uncle Siwei's house were wide open. Looking from outside the door, one could clearly see the verdant oleanders planted on both sides of the courtyard. Hanging in the main hall was a large red satin banner embroidered with the "Eight Immortals", and red candles were burning. It looked like a New Year celebration, but there was also a band of musicians playing and drumming incessantly. This made the onlookers guess that Uncle Siwei's family must have a happy occasion today.

"Get out of my face! Today is my lucky day. Don't try to get me to give out lucky money! ... I don't have that much spare money to support you, you good-for-nothing. I've already supported you for over ten years, and you can't even do any work. You can't even give me a son... Damn it, get out of my sight! ... If you don't leave, I'll..."

Uncle Siwei, who had a flat nose, was wearing a brand new water-green silk cotton robe, topped with a black satin waistcoat. Although he was a middle-aged man, this outfit made him look at least a few years younger. He angrily raised his voice and cursed, and at the same time, personally dragged a middle-aged woman with messy, disheveled hair out the door.

The middle-aged woman sobbed sorrowfully, her eyes swollen and red like two overripe walnuts, her face covered with a silvery, paper-like pallor, barely resembling a living person. She sat on the stone steps at the door, her head hanging low, like hanging in front of her chest, crying like a child, mumbling unintelligible words.

The neighbors, men and women, abandoned their work and, with curious eyes, came to watch the spectacle, their backs against each other, chests against backs, surrounding her heavily, a sense of injustice and pity flowing through everyone's hearts.

"What's wrong, Aunt Siwei? What happened at home?" Aunt Houfu, nicknamed Nosy-Mouth, squeezed out of the crowd, her lips long and pointed like a rat's mouth, squatting down and pulling at the corner of Aunt Siwei's clothes.

"It's... because... I'm getting... old, not... pretty. So, that... old bastard said I... can't bear sons, so... he's abandoning me to take... a younger, more... seductive girl!" Aunt Siwei said between sobs, her throat hoarse as if pressed down by a heavy stone.

"That's outrageous! Heartless, immortal thing, you can't even have children yourself and you dare to blame others. When you were young, you flattened your nose whoring. You're lucky to still be alive, and you still dare to hope for a son!" Someone interjected from the crowd, cursing.

"Why don't you go tell the village chief and ask him to reason with Uncle Siwei? What's the use of crying?"

Aunt Houfu, the nosy one, finally made this suggestion to her.

"What's the point of telling the village chief? The village chief is fundamentally the same kind of person. Didn't he do the same thing himself before? Women who can't bear children must be abandoned like broken shoes. It's almost become a custom in the village. What's the point of telling him?" Old Man Lin San said with a sigh, then left the crowd, leaning on his crutch.

Most people seemed to know that this tragedy had no ending and scattered like birds, leaving Aunt Siwei alone, sitting on the stone steps, sobbing and constantly pulling up her sleeves to wipe away the tears welling up in her eyes.

Ancient Prose 241

Wang Bingmei Donglai Bo Yi

Huaxing (1260) 9:00 AM to 10:00 AM

Improper Rituals in Alliances and Diplomatic Meetings (Continued)

Now examining the records of Zuo Zhuan, the courteous interactions, the gestures of yielding and greeting, can be enumerated, can be pointed out, appearing throughout the records, this principle is incomprehensible. Alas, I understand it now! All people who desire to deceive the world and sell treachery, always do good in the sight of others, and do evil in the sight of those who do not see. Why not look back at oneself and take a close analogy? If the liver is diseased, the eyes cannot see; if the kidney is diseased, the ears cannot hear; if the spleen is diseased, the mouth cannot eat; if the heart is diseased, the tongue cannot speak. Disease that is unseen by others, will inevitably manifest in what is seen by others. Therefore, the hidden and the revealed, the obscure and the clear, are fundamentally not two different principles. What is hidden is stored up to be revealed, what is obscured is accumulated to be made clear. Those dukes, marquises, high officials of the Spring and Autumn period, never devoted themselves to the study of the dark room and leaking roof. When the time came for alliances and diplomatic meetings, even if they wanted to force themselves to pretend, there was eventually a time when they could not hide it. They forgot even when smearing blood, and did not realize they forgot. Those who became lazy after receiving the fifth degree did not realize their laziness. Those who sighed while playing music did not realize their sighs. Those who followed while talking did not realize their tears. Wearing a square cap, with jangling pendants, solemn and dignified, they believed themselves to be acting in accordance with ritual, but they did not know that people were already criticizing them behind their backs.

Shenbao Local Supplement Movie Special

Grace Moore Says, "I Once Made a Living by Singing for Supper" 243

— Yi Ji

There is no need here to write a short biography of Grace Moore, the most popular American singer of our time, or to recount her life's story. Simply put, she was not born into a humble family, nor was she a noble lady from a prominent household. Yet, she transformed herself from an unknown woman who wasn't worth a penny into a world-renowned figure. "Not worth a penny" is not an exaggeration, because from a young age, she was determined to study opera, but her father resolutely opposed it. She then resolutely abandoned the comfortable life at home to pursue what her heart desired.

Her decision to leave her family was not a rash act. On the contrary, she loved her family very much and found it difficult to leave them. However, one night when she could no longer bear it, because she wanted to follow the call of her own heart and yet obey her strict father's orders, she went alone to the mountaintop. In that place where heaven and earth met, in that silent midnight hour, she pondered and sought to find which path to take. She lay on her back on a large rock at the highest peak of the mountain, with a sky full of stars above her and the conflict between personal freedom and family love raging in her heart. She lay there until the east gradually turned pale, and the stars disappeared one by one, before slowly returning home. She decided that she must follow her own aspirations, and as for family love, she would find a way to restore it after achieving success.

She borrowed three hundred dollars from relatives and friends and set off for New York. She had no friends in New York, nor any pre-arranged work. Yet she went forward without hesitation, never doubting her future, even though she often did not know where her next meal would come from.

She lived in Greenwich Village in the countryside, sharing a sparsely furnished house with three other young women. In the daytime, they would go out early to look for work. The three hundred dollars dwindled and disappeared surprisingly quickly, but because she had a passionate ambition, she was not worried or afraid. Sure enough, she soon found a small position in a small restaurant in Greenwich Village—a singing position.

That small restaurant was called "Black Cat," just like the Italian restaurant where she sang for supper in the play "One Night of Love." At that time, her salary was barely enough for her own expenses and the tuition for the singing and music lessons that she considered essential. But she was not worried at all, because she had already found peace of mind. The three women who lived with her were also like-minded and carefree. She said, "We live for today, and we'll worry about tomorrow when it comes, but we all have soaring ambitions, so we all strive every day, moving towards our respective destinations. With each step forward, we all celebrate together. Many times, we had to evade the landlord because we couldn't pay the rent. We all learned to make one dollar do the work of five. But we maintained a high level of thinking, making each day's life an endless adventure!"

It is very comforting to know that all four of the women who lived with Grace Moore have now achieved considerable status. Besides Grace, one was a typist who later married a royal, and now occupies a very high position in European society; one is a dancer who is now famous throughout the world; and one is a sculptor who has not only won great fame in the art world but has also been worshipped by many men, two of whom committed suicide because their marriage proposals were rejected. These four musketeers still often correspond or meet in person. Doesn't this prove that anyone who strives with determination can achieve a considerable position in society?

As for what happened later, the years of struggle, as we mentioned above, we do not intend to write a short biography of her, so there is no need to elaborate. What we want to say is that her ambition to perform at the Metropolitan Opera House, the largest opera house in New York, was not achieved overnight. She went through countless hardships in singing and dancing training and in the struggles of life, but she said, "The ambition I held was not an empty dream. I never lost faith in my own abilities. If I doubted my own abilities, if I had to take a winding path in the course of advancement, and thought that I could not reach my goal, then I would have failed long ago. A person who is worried and depressed because of twists and turns and difficulties is unlikely to succeed."

She also said, "I have seen many people struggling anxiously to fulfill their aspirations, and I feel very sorry for them. Anxious struggle cannot last long. A person's mental energy is limited. If it has been eroded by anxiety, then how can there be any energy left to struggle? Therefore, to struggle, one must have freedom of body and mind, and not be entangled by worries. A person who lowers his head on the battlefield is bound to fail!"

In fact, Grace Moore grew up in the mountains of Tennessee. Therefore, she also has the following words: "I want to live on the mountaintop. I am permanently living on the mountaintop, whether physically or mentally. We can create our own mountaintop. On the mountaintop, we can see our dreams unfolding before our eyes. The most important thing is that we must see how many fragments our dreams are made of, and how success is also made of many fragments. Each fragment is an important part. Each fragment is worth fighting for. If I had not sung for supper, I might not have been able to perform at the Metropolitan Opera House."

Film Reviews

Review of "The President Vanishes" 244

— Ji Han

The President Vanishes - Cathay

Because many recent American films have used World War II as their main theme, we can see that the American people are indeed in a state of anxiety. In "The President Vanishes," the playwright raises the question of whether the United States should participate in the war when it breaks out. Thus, in the play, he assumes that the war has already begun in Europe, and some arms dealers or gray shirts (representing Fascists), using the slogan of preserving America's dignity, advocate participation in the war in newspapers. However, on the other hand, mothers who lost their sons in the First World War cannot help but feel infinite grief. At the same time, the playwright concludes in the mouth of the president at the end: Although the war debts of the United States cannot be recovered (which is used as an excuse to participate in the war), these war debts can never compensate for the blood shed by millions of soldiers.

Obviously, the playwright is anti-war. He believes that the quarrels of a group of arms dealers or politicians for personal gain are nothing more than a group of ducks chattering incessantly. Because a hysterical young man pours leftover wine on the Statue of Liberty to express his hatred, and then points out the theme of non-war in the mouth of the assumed national leader, we cannot help but be awed by his humanitarian righteousness. However, what can he do to curb this strong atmosphere of war? He makes the president hide, rumors are spread that he was kidnapped by arms dealers or Fascist thugs, so that the people of the whole country shift their target and hate the pro-war Fascists, and finally designs to kill the leader of the right wing. Clearly, this is not a solution. As the playwright says, there are many treacherous capitalists in the United States who are creating this war that destroys human civilization. The imperialist American government will never fail to participate in the Second World War and be one of the main members. The humanitarian president who supports peace in the play is ultimately just a well-intentioned fantasy figure of the playwright. On the one hand, he touches the essence of imperialist war to a certain extent, and on the other hand, he entrusts the theme to fantasy, which is either cowardice to escape reality or a lack of in-depth understanding of reality. Precisely because imperialist war is hindering human progress and destroying civilization, then only by using a historically decisive war to eliminate imperialist war, only after the final war can we guarantee the permanent peace of mankind. However, it must be said that when the clouds of war are permeating the entire world, even humanitarian non-war has its minimum significance.

After watching this film, we feel that its script is disorganized, and its structure is not well-organized. However, in some individual scenes, William A. Wellman's direction is very delicate and thoughtful, and several actors who play arms dealers also perform very well. However, in terms of tone, it just raises the plot and then suddenly falls down, failing to create a big wave from several small waves, that is, there is no main center of gravity as the climax of the play. Thus, we only see the scattered individual existence of each scene, without a general convergence. Moreover, the progress of the play becomes even more obscure in the second half, although the first half is quite brilliant. However, the director has indeed worked hard, and the main fault should be borne by the screenwriter. The form is not enough for the content, this film can be an example.

Review of "Music in the Air" 245

— Hua Lun

Music in the Air - Da Guangming Cinema

From the appearance of the colors, "Music in the Air" is indeed a "lively" film. There is the cast of Gloria Swanson and John Boles, there are the songs of Kern and O. Hammerstein, there are the scenes of clear singing and wonderful dancing, and there is the intention of Joe May, the director who is not "rigid." However, if you examine the content, then this so-called "liveliness" will inevitably disappoint you. Besides telling you a cliché love story of a quadrangle, it is a sermon on being optimistic and enjoying the life of "celestial music and wonderful dancing."

The screenwriter also knows that such empty content is not easy to please, so, like the producers of all such films, they stubbornly cast the female lead as a famous actress in order to support the film with singing. In addition, they add comical acting and humorous dialogue to regulate the throat when tired of singing.

The director, who follows this screenwriting method, is also troubled by the lack of room to show his talents. Their power can be seen in the concise and powerful editing used for the tranquility of the countryside and the troubles of the city. Thus, he opens up delicate techniques and pursues light and witty interests. Due to the proper use of small movements, considerable success has been achieved in this regard. It should be especially mentioned that the two scenes of writing Carl in the countryside, the former using birds as an insertion, not only write out the innocence of the child and the life of the teacher Carl, but also cleverly introduce and portray the personality and mood of Ward at that time. The latter uses the tranquility of the countryside to reflect the mood in which Carl is going to the city to find Xiling. These are all successful grasps of the mood.

John Boles's stability and sophistication and the warm emotions of human nature, and Swanson's willful performance, have all reached their respective realms.

Butterfly, Gu Meijun, and Xu Xinfu's new star film "Beauty's Heart" directed will be screened at Xinguang from the 21st of this month.

Novel Film

Clive of India (5) 249

— Mao De

While Clive was putting on the clean clothes that Captain Clark had brought, he said slowly, "I crawled in the enemy's lines for three days and three nights, enduring hardships and hunger, just to see you?" Manning said impatiently, "Then what is it? Tell me quickly!" Clive said, "Give me all the men. I'll relieve the siege of De Linapur." Governor Pigot frowned and told him that there were only one hundred and twenty men under his command now. Clive said, "That's enough."

Cand asked, "De Linapur has five hundred men and still can't relieve themselves. How can you relieve them with one hundred and twenty men?" Clive put on his clean socks and boots unhurriedly and said slowly, "Isn't that easy? I just won't go there." Warburton shouted, "Then how can you relieve their siege?" Clive said, "I'll attack Arcot." Warburton said, "Attack Arcot? Attack the capital of southern India with one hundred and twenty men?" He thought this was simply the dream of a madman.

But Governor Pigot understood his meaning. Although this was a near-mad act, but things had come to this, madness might point out a way out. He suddenly thought that there should be a few more madmen at this time. At this time, Clive was still explaining with a sarcastic tone: "If the enemy's strength is greater than yours, your only way is to divide them, and then divide them again, and then break them one by one. But you don't understand this. You don't have to worry about it either. Leave it to me. Also, gentlemen, you have no other way to go. Sitting here is waiting to be slaughtered. Now there is only one sentence, do you want me to do this?"

Governor Pigot rose up and said, "I unconditionally agree." Clive acknowledged the location of true authority, bowed to Pigot, and then turned around and instructed Captain Clark, "Gather all the men together—the lame, the blind, the sick, the drunk, the sober, all of them!" Captain Clark happily said, "Yes, sir!" He saluted smartly, then turned around and strode out.

Manning asked again, "Then when will you lead this madman team to set off?" Clive said, "Right now." He stood up and was about to follow Clark out. Suddenly he stopped again and asked, "Forgot the most important thing! Is there any letter from home?" Warburton said, "There are letters, but unfortunately the ship was captured by the French, and we didn't receive them here." Clive walked out while saying hatefully, "A bunch of fools. They only know how to sit on their tails and doze off. Letting my letter be robbed by the French!"

He reviewed his "army," the general people that Captain Clark had hastily gathered. He thought to himself, what a beggar team. But he knew that if he wanted to use them, he must first arouse their spirit and encourage their courage. He deliberately said loudly, "Captain, where did all these strong men come from! Excellent! You can't ask for better!" With just a few words, he had already created a small miracle. These many listless people actually stretched their shoulders flat, raised their heads high, and straightened their waists. Everyone felt in their hearts that with such an officer, the impossible was also possible. Clive asked the drummer boy, "What orders can you blow?" He said, "Attention, raise gun, stop, retreat—and go forward." Clive said, "I only want the last one—go——forward!" That team of mixed people had already set off. (To be continued)

Shen Bao Local Supplement Automobile Weekly

The Newest 1935 Eight-Cylinder Ford 250

— Hua

The most obvious features of the new eight-cylinder Ford are its new body style and unique construction. In terms of mechanics, it adopts the "center of gravity" principle of riding, so the ride is more comfortable. As for its chassis, there are also many improvements that make management easier. There are now 1.3 million of these newest Ford cars on the road.

After three years of continuous effort and research, the Ford factory has achieved this newest eight-cylinder car. Its ease of driving, comfortable ride, and novel structure are unmatched. It is the crystallization of careful improvement.

In terms of appearance, it has a fresh image and beautiful curves, suitable for modern tastes. The interior and all the equipment have also been carefully managed, making the body style of the new Ford perfect.

The progress of its engine and chassis is no less important than the car style. Among them, the most important feature is its adoption of a new spring suspension system. Also, the weight of the car and passengers is properly distributed, so that the passenger position can be in the center of the car, which is called "center of gravity" riding. Passengers ride between the wheels. In order to achieve this goal, the front car spring is lengthened and positioned more than four inches in front of the front axle, and the engine is moved more than eight inches forward, so that its importance is entrusted to the front axle. Both the front and rear springs can be stretched more than before. Also, due to the improvement of the front end of the chassis, the chassis position is more spacious, so the load weight can be redistributed to concentrate in the middle of the four wheels. Therefore, the weight entrusted to the two axles can be approximately equal, and the comfort of the rear seat passengers is no different from sitting in the front seat.

As for the reform of its external structure, the repositioning of the front spring engine is the main focus. The body can therefore be moved to the front, and passengers can sit in the middle of the axle. The rear mirror panel can also be arranged in a streamlined style. Between the mutual bumpers, the car is about eight inches longer.

Other things such as the engine car, the front window glass, and the mudguards are also new and beautiful.

Also, its wheels are smaller and its tires are larger, so there is no suffering from bumps when driving on rugged roads.

Speaking of the interior of the new Ford, its position is more spacious. Both the front and rear seats are widened. The front seat is widened by five and a half inches, which can accommodate three people without feeling crowded. The driver's seat has active devices on the sedan. The soft pads and all the equipment are suitable.

As for the engine, there are also many improvements. A DC crankcase ventilation device is installed, which can make the water vapor and gas emitted from the crankcase and valve chamber completely removed. Therefore, the residual water accumulated in the gasoline can be reduced to a minimum, and the formation of sludge and the dilution of gasoline are also reduced, which can extend the life of gasoline and reduce engine damage.

Also, the aircraft-style copper-lead connecting rod bearings are the same as those used on high-speed racing cars and aircraft engines. They are all designed to withstand hard work without any risk of being unreliable.

Also, its alloy cast camshaft is also new.

The brakes of the new Ford are of the latest style. They adopt an internal expansion style, which is intended to give a more effective braking function, and the foot force can be reduced. There is also a new type of sliding tip, which is part of its construction, which is to average the pressure. Its connector is new and simple. When starting and shifting gears, it requires less force and the action is quiet. At high speeds, the pressure is increased due to centrifugal force, which increases the original force and shifting ability of the connector.

Its connector is new and simple. When starting and shifting gears, it requires less force and the action is quiet. At high speeds, the pressure is increased due to centrifugal force, which increases the original force and shifting ability of the connector.

As for the new and solid frame, the stable front and rear struts, the widened rear wheel track, and the strengthened rear axle are also its characteristics.

Austin Expands Overseas Market 251

— Yi

The British Industrial Exhibition is about to open. It is seen that customers from all over the world are still going to it from thousands of miles away. But in this voice, a large British manufacturer is selecting representatives in order to open up the market and promote sales. It is thought that this manufacturer is none other than the famous Austin Motor Company.

Since the factory's business policy has been decided, it specially dispatched an overseas representative by plane to Benma, Singapore, and the Masur Islands last week. Another representative went to China, Japan, and Canada. The third representative contacted all the important commercial centers in the Near East and Southern Europe before returning to Poland. In addition to this, personnel will soon be sent to Northern Europe and Sweden, Norway, and other countries. Because the trade situation in each of these places is good, the increase in Austin sales is very promising.

Therefore, the importance of their mission is the same as that of a British commercial envoy. Last year's Austin export volume increased by 30% compared to the previous year. Now there is such a large-scale activity, so the total Austin export volume in 1935 will be more than that in 1934.

New Trends in 1935 American Car Body Manufacturing 252

— Ying Dai

(1) All-Steel Car Roof

In the past few years, the design of the upper part of cars has been greatly influenced by aircraft streamlining. The 1935 car bodies continue this trend. In fact, car manufacturers have been gradually improving their manufacturing processes and are satisfied with the current state, without seeking complete innovation. At first glance, the 1935 models may not seem much different from the previous year. However, upon closer comparison with the 1934 models, one will notice that the current year's manufacturing emphasizes smooth curves and reduces sharp lines. The most significant innovation in this year's car body manufacturing is the wider exterior and the use of all-steel for the roof. In the past, so-called all-steel car bodies usually had roofs made of fabric and steel wire. However, many of the 1935 models have pure steel roofs from front to back and left to right. One particular manufacturer, a well-known brand, still uses a combination of steel and wood for the car body. While other parts of the car body still contain wooden components, the roof is made entirely of steel.

(2) Front Appearance of the Car

Looking at the front of the car, one can immediately notice that the radiator is longer and narrower than before. This type of radiator was previously only used in high-end cars, but it is now commonly adopted. One car manufacturer has meticulously designed the radiator grille, frame, and shell to create a narrow radiator form. The long and narrow grille and frame are made entirely of chrome. The radiator shell is painted the same color as the car and is moderately wide. To ensure that the heat dissipation effect is not compromised, the curved side of the radiator shell has small, flat line perforations. Inside the radiator shell, narrow, flat line louvers are located at the top. In general, the front of the car is now designed very appropriately. Chrome is used economically for the radiator grille, frame, headlight bezels, and even the bumper guards. The fenders are wider and lower, with mud flaps that conceal the lower part of the chassis. On the running boards and the middle of the car body, the side mud flaps have been removed in some cases to make the car body look smoother and more beautiful.

(3) New Style Windshields

The backs of the front and rear bumper guards have undergone many reforms and designs, all having edges, and some even have defenses attached to cover the upper half of the rear wheels. Radiator shells and windshields were traditionally slanted. This year is the same. The radiator shell is rounder this year. The radiator cap has been moved back, just in front of the car body pillar. Windshields are fixed and adjustable, probably due to the influence of internal air circulation methods. There are many styles for air circulation inside the car, and there have been past successes. Double-piece windshields are installed diagonally in a V-shape to divert airflow. Some car manufacturers, to improve the ventilation on the roof, exhaust the heat from under the chassis by opening louvers under the fenders or engine side panels. At least one car manufacturer uses laminated glass for the windshield, with the middle piece spanning the entire width of the car, taking up a lot of space, and two smaller pieces attached on both sides, taking up

Greek Queen Orders a 1935 Studebaker 253

— Fu

The local Da Xia Automobile Company recently received a telegram from the Studebaker factory stating that at the opening of this year's New York Auto Show, Queen Elisabeth of Greece purchased a Studebaker President Twelve, 175 horsepower, Arrow brand sedan with a wheelbase of 144 inches. The car will be painted deep black, in contrast to the all-white, gold-trimmed Arrow car commissioned by the King of Persia. The only exterior ornament on the car is a small silver crown affixed to the center of both rear doors. In addition, a hole for a flagpole must be drilled in the front left fender.

The interior upholstery must be luxurious and must include a special radio with the speaker hidden at the top of the privacy window. Spare tires and chrome wheels must be installed on the front fenders. The Arrow car's most famous fender headlights of the last ten years are essential.

However, apart from specific equipment, everything else is identical to other Arrow top-of-the-line twelve-cylinder sedans.

Some manufacturers have adopted steep car roofs this year. In this case, the car body looks like a pure steel box, with the top and body sections completely welded together without using nails. Overall, the car neck extends and stretches under the roof, so the car body structure is very strong. In recent years, the car industry has been using all-steel car bodies solely because external vibrations often cause cars to shake and make noise. By selecting materials that insulate against vibration, this external vibration is now completely eliminated.

(4) Safety Glass

Some car manufacturers use safety glass for the entire car body, while others only use safety glass for the windshield and wind deflectors. If the car owner wants to install safety glass throughout the car, they have to pay extra. However, in the United States, road regulations require all new cars to use safety glass starting in 1935. Each year, the progress made in engine manufacturing is sufficient to increase passenger comfort and driver convenience. Advancements in the chassis have made the seats wider, with both front and rear seats enlarged. The legroom inside the car has also been significantly increased. The purpose is to mount the car body on top so that the weight distribution can be more appropriate. Many car bodies have been moved forward this year, allowing passengers to sit in the middle of the axles. At the same time, the engine has been moved forward, placing more of the overall weight on the front axle. The sole purpose of this method is to make both front and rear passengers feel equally comfortable. We recall that in recent years, rear passengers often felt bumps and vibrations because the seats were precisely positioned above the rear axle. However, this will no longer be the case. Both front and rear doors are larger than in previous years. The overall height of this year's new cars has changed little. However, in many vehicles, the space inside the car from the floor to the middle of the roof is significantly wider.

(5) Louvered Windows

The latest louvered windows have become popular this year. They are generally arranged as a row of holes distributed along the entire length of the roof. However, some arrange many short louvered windows in a long row, and even use chrome trim around the louvered windows for decoration, while emphasizing streamlining. Spare tires are hidden in many new cars because a section at the rear can completely cover the tires. The only reason for this is to allow the car manufacturers to make the car body unimpeded to the rear. However, some new cars still use the old method of leaving the spare tire exposed at the rear or placing it in a channel on the side fender. In addition, some new cars combine the rear luggage rack and tire rack, installing hinges so that a tire can be added in addition to luggage. (End)

The Lineup of the British Automotive Industry in 1935 254

— Qin

In recent years, the British automotive industry has shown a firm determination to compete with the American automotive industry. This is particularly evident in 1935. To encourage the automotive industry, the American government decided to reduce the automotive industry tax rate by 20% in 1935 to expand production. The British government also reduced the automotive tax by 20%. Automotive entrepreneurs have also expressed their intention to compete with the United States. Therefore, the British automotive industry in 1935 has a grand plan for development, far from being second to the American automotive industry as it was in the past.

The center of the British automotive industry, the Midlands, is like Detroit in the United States. The various automobile factories in the Midlands are currently in a state of active production. The Standard Motor Company is particularly hard at work. Because sales of Standard cars have increased in the past, the factory does not have enough workers and is recruiting new workers for manufacturing. In addition, the renowned Triumph automobile factory also decided to expand its manufacturing division in 1935 and recruit 30% more new workers. Recruitment has officially begun in London.

Furthermore, the Rolls-Royce Motor Company will also have new developments in 1935. In 1934, the factory's business was very satisfactory, performing better than the previous year, with profits reaching £199,300. The factory is most famous for manufacturing automobile engines. The reason British cars can achieve a considerable position in the world's high-record cars is largely due to the application of engines manufactured by this factory. The factory has a history of 20 years in the British automotive industry and also manufactures marine engines. It is a very comprehensive machinery manufacturing business. In 1935, it will adopt various novel mechanical raw materials. The factory's greatest cylinder manufacturing department has added more than 200 engineers. (To be continued)
